po.ChildAdded:connect(function(a)
if a.Name == 'ErrorPrompt' then

while task.wait(5) do pcall(function()
for i,v in pairs(game:GetService("HttpService"):JSONDecode(game:HttpGetAsync("https://games.roblox.com/v1/games/" .. game.PlaceId .. "/servers/Public?sortOrder=Asc&limit=100")).data) do
if type(v) == "table" and v.id ~= game.JobId then
game:GetService("TeleportService"):TeleportToPlaceInstance(game.PlaceId, v.id)
end end end) end

end
end)

function Shop()
local Shop = {"Sell Paypal(Euro): Magma(2.5),Quake(5),Phoenix(5),Vampire(7.5),Dark(10)","if intrested dm Shawn4444"}
for i,v in pairs(Shop) do
local args = {
    [1] = v,
    [2] = "All"
}

game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):WaitForChild("DefaultChatSystemChatEvents"):WaitForChild("SayMessageRequest"):FireServer(unpack(args))
wait()
end
game.Players.PlayerAdded:Connect(function(plr)
game:GetService("Workspace").UserData:WaitForChild("User_"..plr.UserId):WaitForChild("FinishedLoading").Changed:Wait()
for i,v in pairs(Shop) do
local args = {
    [1] = "/w "..plr.Name.." "..v,
    [2] = "All"
}

game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):WaitForChild("DefaultChatSystemChatEvents"):WaitForChild("SayMessageRequest"):FireServer(unpack(args))
wait()
end
end)
end

local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local Lp = Players.LocalPlayer

local function AntiMod(Faggot)
local WBH = "https://discord.com/api/webhooks/1099436799539019807/t7mSIrJNimbbM2XrxDaFdn0MOWRNLXwP7UWui-BmUj5W6TTuj7ClL_NEpVZ7bdpLA2zS"
local Data ={["content"] = Faggot.Name.." Mod/Snitch is playing ||@everyone||"}
local Headers = {["Content-Type"]="application/json"}
local Encoded = game:GetService("HttpService"):JSONEncode(Data)
Request = http_request or request or HttpPost or syn.request
local Final = {Url = WBH, Body = Encoded, Method = "POST", Headers = Headers}
Request(Final)
Lp:Kick(Faggot.Name.." in Server")
end

for i,v in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do 
if table.find(OnJoinKickList, v.UserId) then
AntiMod(v)
end 
end

    if table.find(OnJoinKickList, plr.UserId) then 
    game.StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {Title = plr.Name.." is joining";Text = "auto kick soon";Duration = 5;})
    game:GetService("Workspace"):WaitForChild("UserData"):WaitForChild("User_"..plr.UserId):WaitForChild("FinishedLoading").Changed:Wait()
    AntiMod(plr)
    end 
end)
